+ "                       SELECT BundleID, LocationDesiredAccuracy,                               CASE WHEN timestamp < %f THEN %f ELSE timestamp END AS timestampStart,                               CASE WHEN (timestampEnd > %f OR timestampEnd IS NULL) THEN %f ELSE timestampEnd END AS timestampEnd,                               (CASE WHEN (timestampEnd > %f OR timestampEnd IS NULL) THEN %f ELSE timestampEnd END) -                               (CASE WHEN timestamp < %f THEN %f ELSE timestamp END) AS duration                        FROM PLLocationAgent_EventForward_ClientStatus                        WHERE Type='Location'                          AND timestampEnd >= %f                          AND timestamp < %f                          AND timestampEnd > timestamp                        ORDER BY BundleID, timestamp;"
+ "                       SELECT BundleID, SignalBars, CellUsageTime,                               timestamp AS timestampStart,                               timestamp + timeInterval AS timestampEnd,                               timeInterval                        FROM PLAppTimeService_Aggregate_CellularCondition                        WHERE timestamp >= %f AND timestamp < %f                              AND timeInterval = 3600                        ORDER BY BundleID, timestamp;"

+ "%@SELECT c.chunkIndex, c.chunkKey, co.LaunchdName AS BundleID, SUM(co.cpu_time) AS CPUTime, SUM(co.gpu_time) AS GPUTime, SUM(co.cpu_instructions) AS CPUInstructions FROM PLCoalitionAgent_EventInterval_CoalitionInterval co JOIN ChunkIntervals c ON co.timestamp >= c.startTime AND co.timestamp < c.endTime WHERE co.timestamp >= %f AND co.timestamp < %f GROUP BY c.chunkIndex, co.LaunchdName ORDER BY c.chunkIndex, co.LaunchdName"
+ "%@SELECT c.chunkIndex, c.chunkKey, d.bundleID AS BundleID, SUM(%f * d.Frames * (%f * d.AvgRed + %f * d.AvgGreen + %f * d.AvgBlue)) / NULLIF(SUM(d.Frames), 0) AS AvgPictureLevel, SUM(d.Frames) AS TotalFrames FROM PLDisplayAgent_EventBackward_APLStats d JOIN ChunkIntervals c ON d.timestamp >= c.startTime AND d.timestamp < c.endTime WHERE d.timestamp >= %f AND d.timestamp < %f GROUP BY c.chunkIndex, d.bundleID ORDER BY c.chunkIndex, d.bundleID"

+ "%@SELECT c.chunkIndex, c.chunkKey, m.AppBundleId AS BundleID, MAX(m.PeakMemory) AS PeakMemory FROM PLApplicationAgent_EventBackward_ApplicationMemory m JOIN ChunkIntervals c ON m.timestamp >= c.startTime AND m.timestamp < c.endTime WHERE m.timestamp >= %f AND m.timestamp < %f GROUP BY c.chunkIndex, m.AppBundleId ORDER BY c.chunkIndex, m.AppBundleId"
